#	uk_post_war_rationing_good_progress						: Master Progress Variable to track number of months good has spent outside the acceptable price range
#	uk_post_war_rationing_good_progress_from_characters		: Variable tracking characters
#	uk_post_war_rationing_good_progress_from_igs			: Variable tracking interest groups
#	uk_post_war_rationing_good_progress_from_buildings		: Variable tracking buildings
#	uk_post_war_rationing_good_progress_from_legitimacy		: Variable tracking current government legitimacy. Strong government = fast progress variable reduction. Weak government legitimacy = slow or no progress variable reduction
#	uk_post_war_rationing_good_progress_from_effects		: Variable tracking effects from events, etc, that influence the progress Variable
#	uk_post_war_rationing_good_progress_from_price			: Variable tracking market price of good
#	uk_post_war_rationing_good_progress_next				: Variable is an incrementor - it is calculated from previous 6 variables (characters, IGs, buildings, government legitimacy, events) on a weekly basis, and is added to uk_post_war_rationing_good_progress on the monthly. Used in localization to tell the player the current rate of change for uk_post_war_rationing_good_progress is.

gbr_set_uk_post_war_rationing_core_variables = {
	# Used solely for mathematical purposes, and is set as equivalent to the clout
	# of a given interest group. It exists so that IGs can be weighted higher or lower
	# depending on whether they're in government or not
	set_variable = { name = uk_ig_weight value = 0 }
	
	# Button Visibility
	set_variable = uk_staple_goods_visible
	set_variable = uk_industrial_goods_visible
	set_variable = uk_luxury_goods_visible
	set_variable = uk_all_goods_visible
	
	# Core Variables
	set_variable = { name = uk_ending_rationing_starting_variable value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_ending_rationing_target_variable value = 6 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_rationing_number_of_goods value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_rationing_inflation_rate value = 2.75 } # UK's 1945 inflation rate
	set_variable = { name = uk_added_inflation value = 0 }
	
	# Progress Variables
	set_variable = { name = gbr_biggest_goods_risk_progress value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_bauxite_progress value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_fertilizer_progress value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_clothes_progress value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_coal_progress value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_coffee_progress value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_copper_progress value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_explosives_progress value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_fabric_progress value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_fish_progress value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_fruit_progress value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_glass_progress value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_grain_progress value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_groceries_progress value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_high_quality_fabric_progress value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_lead_progress value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_liquor_progress value = 0 }

#####################################

# Aluminum rationing progress weekly calculation
gbr_weekly_pulse_uk_rationing_aluminum_progress = {
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_characters value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_igs value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_buildings value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_legitimacy value = root.government_legitimacy }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_effects value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_next value = 0 }
	
	# From Characters - for future reworks if more character interaction is involved in the mod/game
		
	# From Interest Groups - for future reworks if more interest group interaction is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Buildings - for future reworks if more building interactions is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Government Legitimacy
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_legitimacy divide = 100 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_legitimacy subtract = 0.5 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_legitimacy multiply = -1 }
	
	# From price - Price of good goes beyond given limits, government losing control over pricing so progress increases
	#			   Price of good within given limits, government regaining control over pricing so progress decreases
	#			   Easier to lose control than regain it, so takes longer to regain control over pricing of good
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price add = 1 } # = 1
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.25 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price add = 1 } # = 2
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price add = 3 } # = 5
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.45 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price add = 4 } # = 9
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.55 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price add = 6 } # = 15
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.65 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price add = 7 } # = 22
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.75 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price add = 8 } # = 30
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price subtract = 0.5 } # = -0.5
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.25 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price subtract = 0.5 } # = -1
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price subtract = 1.5 } # = -2.5
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.45 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price subtract = 2 } # = -4.5
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.55 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price subtract = 3 } # = -7.5
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.65 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price subtract = 3.5 } # = -11
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.75 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price subtract = 4 } # = -15
	}
	
	# Final Compliiation
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_characters }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_igs }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_buildings }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_legitimacy }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_effects }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress_from_price }
}

# Clothes rationing progress weekly calculation
gbr_weekly_pulse_uk_rationing_clothes_progress = {
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_clothes_progress_from_characters value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_clothes_progress_from_igs value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_clothes_progress_from_buildings value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_clothes_progress_from_legitimacy value = root.government_legitimacy }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_clothes_progress_from_effects value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_clothes_progress_from_price value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_clothes_progress_next value = 0 }
	
	# From Characters - for future reworks if more character interaction is involved in the mod/game
		
	# From Interest Groups - for future reworks if more interest group interaction is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Buildings - for future reworks if more building interactions is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Government Legitimacy
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_clothes_progress_from_legitimacy divide = 100 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_clothes_progress_from_legitimacy subtract = 0.5 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_clothes_progress_from_legitimacy multiply = -1 }
	
	# From price - Price of good goes beyond given limits, government losing control over pricing so progress increases
	#			   Price of good within given limits, government regaining control over pricing so progress decreases
	#			   Easier to lose control than regain it, so takes longer to regain control over pricing of good
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:clothes = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_clothes_progress_from_price add = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:clothes = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.25 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_clothes_progress_from_price add = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:clothes = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_clothes_progress_from_price add = 3 }

		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_clothes_progress_from_price add = 4 }
	}
	if = {

		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_clothes_progress_from_price add = 6 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:clothes = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.65 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_clothes_progress_from_price add = 7 }
	}
	if = {

		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_clothes_progress_from_price add = 8 }

	# From Interest Groups - for future reworks if more interest group interaction is involved in the mod/game

	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_legitimacy subtract = 0.5 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_legitimacy multiply = -1 }
	
	# From price - Price of good goes beyond given limits, government losing control over pricing so progress increases
	#			   Price of good within given limits, government regaining control over pricing so progress decreases
	#			   Easier to lose control than regain it, so takes longer to regain control over pricing of good

		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:engines = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_price add = 1 }

		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_price add = 3 }

		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_price add = 4 }
	}
	if = {

		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_price add = 6 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:engines = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.65 } } }

		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_price add = 8 }
	}

		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_engines_progress_from_price subtract = 0.5 }

	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_fruit_progress_from_effects value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_fruit_progress_from_price value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_fruit_progress_next value = 0 }
	
	# From Characters - for future reworks if more character interaction is involved in the mod/game
		
	# From Interest Groups - for future reworks if more interest group interaction is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Buildings - for future reworks if more building interactions is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Government Legitimacy
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_fruit_progress_from_legitimacy divide = 100 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_fruit_progress_from_legitimacy subtract = 0.5 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_fruit_progress_from_legitimacy multiply = -1 }
	
	# From price - Price of good goes beyond given limits, government losing control over pricing so progress increases
	#			   Price of good within given limits, government regaining control over pricing so progress decreases
	#			   Easier to lose control than regain it, so takes longer to regain control over pricing of good
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:fruit = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_fruit_progress_from_price add = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:fruit = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.25 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_fruit_progress_from_price add = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:fruit = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_fruit_progress_from_price add = 3 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:fruit = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.45 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_fruit_progress_from_price add = 4 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:fruit = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.55 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_fruit_progress_from_price add = 6 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:fruit = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.65 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_fruit_progress_from_price add = 7 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:fruit = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.75 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_fruit_progress_from_price add = 8 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:fruit = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_fruit_progress_from_price subtract = 0.5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:fruit = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.25 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_fruit_progress_from_price subtract = 0.5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:fruit = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_fruit_progress_from_price subtract = 1.5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:fruit = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.45 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_fruit_progress_from_price subtract = 2 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:fruit = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.55 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_fruit_progress_from_price subtract = 3 }
	}
	if = {

		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_fruit_progress_from_price subtract = 3.5 }

# Iron rationing progress weekly calculation
gbr_weekly_pulse_uk_rationing_iron_progress = {
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_characters value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_igs value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_buildings value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_legitimacy value = root.government_legitimacy }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_effects value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_next value = 0 }
	
	# From Characters - for future reworks if more character interaction is involved in the mod/game
		
	# From Interest Groups - for future reworks if more interest group interaction is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Buildings - for future reworks if more building interactions is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Government Legitimacy
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_legitimacy divide = 100 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_legitimacy subtract = 0.5 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_legitimacy multiply = -1 }
	
	# From price - Price of good goes beyond given limits, government losing control over pricing so progress increases
	#			   Price of good within given limits, government regaining control over pricing so progress decreases
	#			   Easier to lose control than regain it, so takes longer to regain control over pricing of good
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price add = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.25 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price add = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price add = 3 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.45 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price add = 4 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.55 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price add = 6 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.65 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price add = 7 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.75 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price add = 8 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price subtract = 0.5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.25 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price subtract = 0.5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price subtract = 1.5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.45 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price subtract = 2 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.55 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price subtract = 3 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.65 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price subtract = 3.5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:iron = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.75 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_price subtract = 4 }
	}
	
	# Final Compliiation
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_characters }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_igs }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_iron_progress_from_buildings }

# Oil rationing progress weekly calculation
gbr_weekly_pulse_uk_rationing_oil_progress = {
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_characters value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_igs value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_buildings value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_legitimacy value = root.government_legitimacy }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_effects value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_next value = 0 }
	
	# From Characters - for future reworks if more character interaction is involved in the mod/game
		
	# From Interest Groups - for future reworks if more interest group interaction is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Buildings - for future reworks if more building interactions is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Government Legitimacy
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_legitimacy divide = 100 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_legitimacy subtract = 0.5 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_legitimacy multiply = -1 }
	
	# From price - Price of good goes beyond given limits, government losing control over pricing so progress increases
	#			   Price of good within given limits, government regaining control over pricing so progress decreases
	#			   Easier to lose control than regain it, so takes longer to regain control over pricing of good
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price add = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.25 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price add = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price add = 3 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.45 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price add = 4 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.55 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price add = 6 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.65 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price add = 7 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.75 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price add = 8 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price subtract = 0.5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.25 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price subtract = 0.5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price subtract = 1.5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.45 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price subtract = 2 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.55 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price subtract = 3 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.65 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price subtract = 3.5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:oil = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.75 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_price subtract = 4 }
	}
	
	# Final Compliiation
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_characters }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_igs }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_oil_progress_from_buildings }

	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_phosphorus_progress_next value = 0 }

	# From Interest Groups - for future reworks if more interest group interaction is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Buildings - for future reworks if more building interactions is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Government Legitimacy
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_phosphorus_progress_from_legitimacy divide = 100 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_phosphorus_progress_from_legitimacy subtract = 0.5 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_phosphorus_progress_from_legitimacy multiply = -1 }
	
	# From price - Price of good goes beyond given limits, government losing control over pricing so progress increases
	#			   Price of good within given limits, government regaining control over pricing so progress decreases
	#			   Easier to lose control than regain it, so takes longer to regain control over pricing of good

	}

		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:phosphorus = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.25 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_phosphorus_progress_from_price add = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:phosphorus = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_phosphorus_progress_from_price add = 3 }
	}

		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_phosphorus_progress_from_price add = 4 }

	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:phosphorus = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.55 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_phosphorus_progress_from_price add = 6 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:phosphorus = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.65 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_phosphorus_progress_from_price add = 7 }

	if = {

		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_phosphorus_progress_from_price add = 8 }

	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:phosphorus = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_phosphorus_progress_from_price subtract = 0.5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:phosphorus = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.25 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_phosphorus_progress_from_price subtract = 0.5 }

	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:phosphorus = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_phosphorus_progress_from_price subtract = 1.5 }

# Sugar rationing progress weekly calculation
gbr_weekly_pulse_uk_rationing_sugar_progress = {
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_characters value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_igs value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_buildings value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_legitimacy value = root.government_legitimacy }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_effects value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_price value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_next value = 0 }
	
	# From Characters - for future reworks if more character interaction is involved in the mod/game
		
	# From Interest Groups - for future reworks if more interest group interaction is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Buildings - for future reworks if more building interactions is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Government Legitimacy
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_legitimacy divide = 100 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_legitimacy subtract = 0.5 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_legitimacy multiply = -1 }
	
	# From price - Price of good goes beyond given limits, government losing control over pricing so progress increases
	#			   Price of good within given limits, government regaining control over pricing so progress decreases
	#			   Easier to lose control than regain it, so takes longer to regain control over pricing of good
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:sugar = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_price add = 1 }
	}

		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:sugar = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.25 } } }

		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_price add = 4 }
	}
	if = {

		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_price add = 6 }
	}
	if = {

		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_price add = 7 }

		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_sugar_progress_from_price add = 8 }

		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:tools = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_from_price subtract = 1.5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:tools = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.45 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_from_price subtract = 2 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:tools = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.55 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_from_price subtract = 3 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:tools = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.65 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_from_price subtract = 3.5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:tools = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.75 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_from_price subtract = 4 }
	}
	
	# Final Compliiation
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_from_characters }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_from_igs }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_from_buildings }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_from_legitimacy }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_from_effects }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_tools_progress_from_price }
}

# Wine rationing progress weekly calculation
gbr_weekly_pulse_uk_rationing_wine_progress = {
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_characters value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_igs value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_buildings value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_legitimacy value = root.government_legitimacy }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_effects value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price value = 0 }
	set_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_next value = 0 }
	
	# From Characters - for future reworks if more character interaction is involved in the mod/game
		
	# From Interest Groups - for future reworks if more interest group interaction is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Buildings - for future reworks if more building interactions is involved in the mod/game
	
	# From Government Legitimacy
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_legitimacy divide = 100 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_legitimacy subtract = 0.5 }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_legitimacy multiply = -1 }
	
	# From price - Price of good goes beyond given limits, government losing control over pricing so progress increases
	#			   Price of good within given limits, government regaining control over pricing so progress decreases
	#			   Easier to lose control than regain it, so takes longer to regain control over pricing of good
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price add = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.25 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price add = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price add = 3 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.45 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price add = 4 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.55 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price add = 6 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.65 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price add = 7 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.75 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price add = 8 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.15 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price subtract = 0.5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.25 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price subtract = 0.5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.35 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price subtract = 1.5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.45 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price subtract = 2 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.55 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price subtract = 3 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.65 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price subtract = 3.5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { market_capital.market = { mg:wine = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.75 } } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price subtract = 4 }
	}
	
	# Final Compliiation
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_characters }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_igs }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_buildings }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_legitimacy }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_effects }
	change_variable = { name = uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_next add = var:uk_post_war_rationing_wine_progress_from_price }
}

gbr_start_rationing_aluminum = {
	# Check that the UK is rationing & not already rationing aluminum
	# Determine whether aluminum needs to be rationed
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_variable = uk_started_rationing
			market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_buy_orders >= 25 } }
			market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_pricier >= 0.1 } }
			NOT = { has_variable = uk_rationing_aluminum }
		}
		set_variable = uk_rationing_aluminum
		gbr_set_uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_variables = yes
		post_notification = gbr_aluminum_rationing_started_message
	}
}

gbr_end_rationing_aluminum = {
	# Check to see if rationing for aluminum can be ended
	# aluminum has to be 20% cheaper than base price for 6 months in a row
	if = {
		limit = {
			market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.1 } }
			var:uk_ending_aluminum_rationing < var:uk_ending_rationing_target_variable
		}
		change_variable = { name = uk_ending_aluminum_rationing add = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.1 } } }
			var:uk_ending_aluminum_rationing <= var:uk_ending_rationing_target_variable
		}
		set_variable = { name = uk_ending_aluminum_rationing value = 0 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			market_capital.market = { mg:aluminum = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.1 } }
			var:uk_ending_aluminum_rationing = var:uk_ending_rationing_target_variable
		}
		post_notification = gbr_aluminum_rationing_ended_message
		remove_variable = uk_rationing_aluminum
		gbr_remove_uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_variables = yes
	}
}

gbr_end_rationing_bauxite = {
	# Check to see if rationing for bauxite can be ended
	# bauxite has to be 20% cheaper than base price for 6 months in a row
	if = {
		limit = {
			market_capital.market = { mg:bauxite = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.1 } }
			var:uk_ending_bauxite_rationing < var:uk_ending_rationing_target_variable
		}
		change_variable = { name = uk_ending_bauxite_rationing add = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { market_capital.market = { mg:bauxite = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.1 } } }
			var:uk_ending_bauxite_rationing <= var:uk_ending_rationing_target_variable
		}
		set_variable = { name = uk_ending_bauxite_rationing value = 0 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			market_capital.market = { mg:bauxite = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.1 } }
			var:uk_ending_bauxite_rationing = var:uk_ending_rationing_target_variable
		}
		post_notification = gbr_bauxite_rationing_ended_message
		remove_variable = uk_rationing_bauxite
		gbr_remove_uk_post_war_rationing_bauxite_variables = yes
	}
}

			var:uk_ending_opium_rationing < var:uk_ending_rationing_target_variable
		}
		change_variable = { name = uk_ending_opium_rationing add = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { market_capital.market = { mg:opium = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.1 } } }
			var:uk_ending_opium_rationing <= var:uk_ending_rationing_target_variable
		}
		set_variable = { name = uk_ending_opium_rationing value = 0 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			market_capital.market = { mg:opium = { market_goods_cheaper >= 0.1 } }
			var:uk_ending_opium_rationing = var:uk_ending_rationing_target_variable
		}
		post_notification = gbr_opium_rationing_ended_message
		remove_variable = uk_rationing_opium
		gbr_remove_uk_post_war_rationing_opium_variables = yes
	}
}

gbr_forced_devaluation_check = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate >= 70
			var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate < 80
		}
		random_list = {
			99 = {  }
			1 = { trigger_event = united_kingdom_post_war_events.101 }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate >= 80
			var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate < 90
		}
		random_list = {
			95 = {  }
			5 = { trigger_event = united_kingdom_post_war_events.101 }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate >= 90
			var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate < 100
		}
		random_list = {
			90 = {  }
			10 = { trigger_event = united_kingdom_post_war_events.101 }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate >= 100 }
		trigger_event = united_kingdom_post_war_events.101
	}
}

gbr_rationing_inflation_effect = {
	remove_modifier = gbr_goods_demand_deflation
	remove_modifier = gbr_goods_demand_inflation
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate >= 5
			var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate < 10
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = gbr_goods_demand_inflation
			multiplier = 5
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate >= 10
			var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate < 15
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = gbr_goods_demand_inflation
			multiplier = 15
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate >= 15
			var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate < 20
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = gbr_goods_demand_inflation
			multiplier = 25
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate >= 20
			var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate < 25
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = gbr_goods_demand_inflation
			multiplier = 35
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate >= 25
			var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate < 30
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = gbr_goods_demand_inflation
			multiplier = 50
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate >= 30
			var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate < 50
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = gbr_goods_demand_inflation
			multiplier = 60
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate >= 50
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = gbr_goods_demand_inflation
			multiplier = 75
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate < 0
			var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate >= -5
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = gbr_goods_demand_deflation
			multiplier = 5
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate < -5
			var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate >= -10
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = gbr_goods_demand_deflation
			multiplier = 50
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { var:uk_rationing_inflation_rate < -10 }
		add_modifier = {
			name = gbr_goods_demand_deflation
			multiplier = 100
		}
	}
}

gbr_rationing_inflation_change = {
	# What effect does the progress of each good have on the UK's inflation
	set_variable = { name = uk_added_inflation value = 0 }
	if = {
		limit = { has_variable = uk_rationing_aluminum }
		if = {
			limit = { var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress = 0 }
			change_variable = { name = uk_added_inflation subtract = 0.025 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress > 0
				var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress <= 60
			}
			change_variable = { name = uk_added_inflation add = 0.025 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress > 60
				var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress <= 120
			}
			change_variable = { name = uk_added_inflation add = 0.05 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress > 120
				var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress <= 180
			}
			change_variable = { name = uk_added_inflation add = 0.1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress > 180
				var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress <= 240
			}
			change_variable = { name = uk_added_inflation add = 0.15 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress > 240
				var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress <= 300
			}
			change_variable = { name = uk_added_inflation add = 0.2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress > 300
				var:uk_post_war_rationing_aluminum_progress <= 360
			}
			change_variable = { name = uk_added_inflation add = 0.25 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_variable = uk_rationing_bauxite }
		if = {
			limit = { var:uk_post_war_rationing_bauxite_progress = 0 }
			change_variable = { name = uk_added_inflation subtract = 0.025 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:uk_post_war_rationing_bauxite_progress > 0
				var:uk_post_war_rationing_bauxite_progress <= 60
			}
			change_variable = { name = uk_added_inflation add = 0.025 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:uk_post_war_rationing_bauxite_progress > 60
				var:uk_post_war_rationing_bauxite_progress <= 120
			}
			change_variable = { name = uk_added_inflation add = 0.05 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:uk_post_war_rationing_bauxite_progress > 120
				var:uk_post_war_rationing_bauxite_progress <= 180
			}
			change_variable = { name = uk_added_inflation add = 0.1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:uk_post_war_rationing_bauxite_progress > 180
				var:uk_post_war_rationing_bauxite_progress <= 240
			}
			change_variable = { name = uk_added_inflation add = 0.15 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {

	if = {

gbr_number_of_goods_rationed = {
	set_variable = { name = uk_rationing_number_of_goods value = 0 }
	if = { # Aluminum
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = uk_rationing_aluminum } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_rationing_number_of_goods add = 1 }
	}
	if = { # Bauxite
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = uk_rationing_bauxite } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_rationing_number_of_goods add = 1 }
	}
	if = { # Fertilizer ( Chemicals }
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = uk_rationing_fertilizer } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_rationing_number_of_goods add = 1 }
	}
	if = { # Clothes
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = uk_rationing_clothes } }
		change_variable = { name = uk_rationing_number_of_goods add = 1 }
	}
	if = { # Coal

		change_variable = { name = uk_rationing_number_of_goods add = 1 }

gbr_rationing_over = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOR = {
				has_variable = uk_rationing_aluminum
				has_variable = uk_rationing_bauxite
				has_variable = uk_rationing_fertilizer
				has_variable = uk_rationing_clothes
				has_variable = uk_rationing_coal
				has_variable = uk_rationing_coffee
				has_variable = uk_rationing_copper
				has_variable = uk_rationing_engines
				has_variable = uk_rationing_explosives
				has_variable = uk_rationing_fabric
				has_variable = uk_rationing_fish
				has_variable = uk_rationing_fruit
				has_variable = uk_rationing_glass
				has_variable = uk_rationing_grain
				has_variable = uk_rationing_groceries
				has_variable = uk_rationing_high_quality_fabric
				has_variable = uk_rationing_iron
				has_variable = uk_rationing_lead
				has_variable = uk_rationing_liquor
				has_variable = uk_rationing_meat
				has_variable = uk_rationing_oil
				has_variable = uk_rationing_opium
				has_variable = uk_rationing_paper
				has_variable = uk_rationing_pharmaceuticals
				has_variable = uk_rationing_phosphorus
				has_variable = uk_rationing_plastics
				has_variable = uk_rationing_refined_fuel
				has_variable = uk_rationing_rubber
				has_variable = uk_rationing_steel
				has_variable = uk_rationing_sugar
				has_variable = uk_rationing_tea
				has_variable = uk_rationing_tobacco
				has_variable = uk_rationing_tools
				has_variable = uk_rationing_wine
				has_variable = uk_rationing_wood
			}
		}
		set_variable = uk_post_war_rationing_over
	}
}

gbr_random_rationing_events_check = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				AND = {	# Winter of 1947
					game_date >= 1946.12.1
					game_date < 1947.1.1
				}
				AND = {	# Winter of 1948
					game_date >= 1947.12.1
					game_date < 1948.1.1
				}
				AND = {	# Winter of 1949
					game_date >= 1948.12.1
					game_date < 1949.1.1
				}
				AND = {	# Winter of 1950
					game_date >= 1949.12.1
					game_date < 1950.1.1
				}
				AND = {	# Winter of 1951
					game_date >= 1950.12.1
					game_date < 1951.1.1
				}
				AND = {	# Winter of 1952
					game_date >= 1951.12.1
					game_date < 1952.1.1
				}
				AND = {	# Winter of 1953
					game_date >= 1952.12.1
					game_date < 1953.1.1
				}
				AND = {	# Winter of 1954
					game_date >= 1953.12.1
					game_date < 1954.1.1
				}
				AND = {	# Winter of 1955
					game_date >= 1954.12.1
					game_date < 1955.1.1
				}
				AND = {	# Winter of 1956
					game_date >= 1955.12.1
					game_date < 1956.1.1
				}
				AND = {	# Winter of 1957
					game_date >= 1956.12.1
					game_date < 1957.1.1
				}
				AND = {	# Winter of 1958
					game_date >= 1957.12.1
					game_date < 1958.1.1
				}
				AND = {	# Winter of 1959
					game_date >= 1958.12.1
					game_date < 1959.1.1
				}
				AND = {	# Winter of 1960
					game_date >= 1959.12.1
					game_date < 1960.1.1
				}
				AND = {	# Winter of 1961
					game_date >= 1960.12.1
					game_date < 1961.1.1
				}
				AND = {	# Winter of 1962
					game_date >= 1961.12.1
					game_date < 1962.1.1
				}
				AND = {	# Winter of 1963
					game_date >= 1962.12.1
					game_date < 1963.1.1
				}
				AND = {	# Winter of 1964
					game_date >= 1963.12.1
					game_date < 1964.1.1
				}
				AND = {	# Winter of 1965
					game_date >= 1964.12.1
					game_date < 1965.1.1
				}
				AND = {	# Winter of 1966
					game_date >= 1965.12.1
					game_date < 1966.1.1
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				has_modifier = gbr_mild_winter_weather
				has_modifier = gbr_moderate_winter_weather
				has_modifier = gbr_severe_winter_weather
				has_modifier = gbr_critical_winter_weather
				has_modifier = gbr_catastrophic_winter_weather
				has_modifier = gbr_winter_weather_money_cost
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			55 = { trigger_event = united_kingdom_post_war_events.102 } # 55% per year - Mild Winter
			30 = { trigger_event = united_kingdom_post_war_events.103 } # 30% per year - Moderate Winter
			10 = { trigger_event = united_kingdom_post_war_events.104 } # 10% per year - Severe Winter
			3 = { trigger_event = united_kingdom_post_war_events.105 } # 4% per year - Critical Winter
			1 = { trigger_event = united_kingdom_post_war_events.106 } # 1% per year - Catastrophic Winter
		}
	}
}
